<h1 class="text-white font-weight-bold">Thingsquare Privacy Policy</h1>
<!-- SVG Bottom Shape -->
<figure class="position-absolute-bottom-0">
<svg height="140px" preserveaspectratio="none" space="preserve" style="margin-bottom: -8px;" viewbox="20 -20 300 100" width="100%" xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">

<!-- Content -->
<div class="p-7 p-md-9">
<div class="mb-7">
<p>
          Thingsquare AB operates a number of Internet and web based
          services. When using any of them, we may collect certain
          personal information from you. This policy attempts to
          explain what information and how we take care of that
          information.
        </p>
<h2>Website visitors</h2>
<p>
          When you visit any of our publicly available websites, we
          generally collect information that your browser provides our
          web server. This data is aggregated with information from
          other visitors to help us understand how to improve our
          products and services. We may also make information that is
          anonymous and aggregated (such as monthly visitors)
          available to third parties or publish it online.
        </p>
<h2>Registered users</h2>
<p>
          If you register for any our services, we collect such
          information that makes it possible for us to deliver the
          services, store preferences and settings, manage security
          and, when applicable, collect payment. This information may
          include your name, address, organization and email
          address. You may always refuse to divulge such information,
          considering that this may prevent you from using certain
          features.
        </p>
<h2>How we protect your information</h2>
<p>
          We do not sell or rent any personally identifiable
          information to anyone. In order to deliver our products and
          services, we may share personally identifiable information
          with our employees, subcontractors and service providers, on
          a strict need-to-know basis. This also means that
          information may be stored outside your home country. We may
          also share your information after a legal request (such as a
          subpoena) from the legal authorities we are subject to.
        </p>
<h2>If you want to delete your data</h2>
<p>
          According to 26  personuppgiftslagen (1998:204) you may,
          free of charge, once every calendar year, by a written,
          undersigned request addressed to us, receive information
          about what personal information of yours that we have
          collected and how they are used. You may also request that
          we correct your personal information.
        </p>
<h2>Cookies</h2>
<p>
          A cookie is a string of information that a website stores on
          a visitors computer, and that the visitors browser
          provides to the website each time the visitor
          returns. Thingsquare uses cookies to help Thingsquare
          identify and track visitors, their usage of Thingsquare
          websites, and their website access preferences. Thingsquare
          visitors who do not wish to have cookies placed on their
          computers should set their browsers to refuse cookies before
          using Thingsquares websites, with the drawback that certain
          features of Thingsquares websites may not function properly
          without the aid of cookies.
        </p>
<h2>Business Transfers</h2>
<p>
          If Thingsquare, or substantially all of its assets, were
          acquired, or in the unlikely event that Thingsquare goes out
          of business or enters bankruptcy, user information would be
          one of the assets that is transferred or acquired by a third
          party. You acknowledge that such transfers may occur, and
          that any acquirer of Thingsquare may continue to use your
          personal information as set forth in this policy.
        </p>
<h2>How changes to this policy are communicated</h2>
<p>
          The current version of this policy is always available from our
          website. Our registered users who have provided a valid email address
          will be notified about any changes through email.
        </p>
<h2>Agreement</h2>
<p>
          By using our services, you accept that we use your information
          according to the above.
        </p>
<p>
          Thingsquare AB<br/>
          Att: Privacy Team<br/>
          Sankt Eriksgatan 117, 4tr<br/>
          113 43 Stockholm<br/>
          Sweden<br/>
          info@thingsquare.com<br/>
          Registration no: 556828-1991<br/>
</p>
</div>
</div>

    $(document).on('ready', function () {
        function loadscript(file, next) {
            var script = document.createElement('script');
            script.type = 'text/javascript';
            script.onload = next;
            script.src = file;
            document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
        }
        setTimeout(function () {
            loadscript('//js.hs-scripts.com/6754200.js');
        }, 1000);

        if ($('#particles').length > 0) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                loadscript('/ab-particles.min.js', function () {

                    $(":root")[0].style.setProperty('--col-particle', 'rgba(55, 125, 255, 0.5)');
                    $(":root")[0].style.setProperty('--col-bg', '#212121');
                    $(":root")[0].style.setProperty('--col-link', 'rgba(123, 223, 252, 0.8)');
                    $(":root")[0].style.setProperty('--col-text', '#ebe7c5');
                    $(":root")[0].style.setProperty('--col-particle-stroke-hover', 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2)');
                    $(":root")[0].style.setProperty('--col-particle-stroke', 'rgba(55, 125, 255, 0.7)');

                    particles(opacity=100, numParticles=10, sizeMultiplier=2, width=1, connections=true, connectionDensity=15, noBounceH=false, noBounceV=false, speed=30, avoidMouse=false, hover=true);
                });

        function shuffle(array) {
            for (var i = array.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
                var j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
                var temp = array[i];
                array[i] = array[j];
                array[j] = temp;
            }
        }

        $.get('/blog/feed.xml', function (xml) {
            var html = '';

            var num = $(xml).find('item').length;
            var i;
            var randomorder = [];
            for (i = 0; i < num; i += 1) {
                randomorder[i] = i;
            }
            shuffle(randomorder);

            var articles = {};
            $(xml).find('item').each(function (index) {
                var title, subtitle, date, link, picture;
                title = $(this).find('title').text();
                subtitle = $(this).find('subtitle').text();
                date = $(this).find('pubDate').text();
                link = $(this).find('link').text();
                picture = $(this).find('picture').text();


                var biglinkhtml = '<div class="col-md-6 col-lg-4 mb-5 mb-lg-0">' +
                    '<article>' +
                    '<a href="' + link + '" class="d-flex align-items-start flex-column blog-image-overlay lazy" data-src="' + picture + '"></a>' +
                    '<div class="bg-white p-5">' +
                    '<small class="d-block text-secondary mb-1">' + moment.utc(new Date(date)).format('MMMM DD, YYYY') + '</small>' +
                    '<h3 class="h6 mb-0">' +
                    '<a href="' + link + '">' + title + '</a>' +
                    '</h3>' +
                    '<small>' + subtitle + '</small>' +
                    '</div>' +
                    '</article>' +
                    '</div>';
                if (index < 3) {
                    html += biglinkhtml;
                }
                if (index === 0) {
                    var url = '/' + link.split('/').slice(3).join('/');
                    $('#most-recent-blog-post').html(
                        '<a href="' + url + '" class="d-flex align-items-start flex-column u-blog-overlay-v1 transition-3d-hover lazy" data-src="' + picture + '">' +
                        '<article class="w-100 text-center p-6">' +
                        '<small class="d-block mb-1 u-text-light">' + moment.utc(new Date(date)).format('MMMM DD, YYYY') + '</small>' +
                        '<h3 class="h4 text-white">' +
                        title +
                        '</h3><div class="mt-4">' +
                        '<strong class="d-block u-text-light mb-2">' +
                        subtitle +
                        '</strong></div></article></a>');
                    $('#most-recent-blog-post-header').html('Latest Article');
                }

                var name = link.split('/').slice(-2)[0];

                articles[name] = { title: title, subtitle: subtitle, date: date, link: link, picture: picture, name: name };

                $('a[data-see-also="' + name + '"]').attr('href', '/blog/articles/' + name + '/');
                $('img[data-see-also="' + name + '"]').attr('src', '/blog/articles/' + name + '/picture.jpg');
                $('span[data-see-also="' + name + '"]').html(title);
                var element = '<a class="media d-flex align-items-center" href="/blog/articles/' + name + '/">' +
                '<div class="u-blog-overlay-v2" style="background-image: url(/blog/articles/' + name +'/picture.jpg);"></div>' +
                '<span class="media-body ml-3">' +
                '<small class="d-block text-white mb-0">' + title + '</small>' +
                '</span>' +
                '</a>';
                $('.u-blog-thumb-v1[data-see-also="' + name + '"]').html(element);

                element = '<a href="/blog/articles/' + name + '/" class="d-flex align-items-start flex-column u-blog-overlay-v1 transition-3d-hover" style="background-image: url(/blog/articles/' + name +'/picture.jpg);">' +
                '<div class="w-100 d-flex justify-content-between mb-3">' +
                '<small class="d-block u-text-light">' + moment.utc(new Date(date)).format('MMMM DD, YYYY') + '</small>' +
                '</div>' +
                '<div class="mt-auto">' +
                '<h5 class="h5 text-white">' +
                title +
                '</h5>' +
                '<p class="u-text-light mb-0">' + subtitle + '</p>' +
                '</div>' +
                '</a>';

                $('.blog-large[data-see-also="' + name + '"]').html(element);

                $('.blog-random-large[data-num="' + randomorder[index] + '"]').html(element);


            });

            $('div.see-also').each(function () {
                var links = $(this).data('see-also').split(',');
                var text = $(this).data('text') || 'See Also';
                var col = $(this).data('col') || 'col-md';
                var classes = 'u-bg-img-hero u-gradient-overlay-half-primary-v1 rounded-pseudo p-3';
                $(this).addClass(classes);
                var html = '<div class="row d-block h6 text-white mb-1 text-center">' +
                           '<span class="u-divider u-divider--xs">' + text +'</span>' +
                           '</div>' +
                           '<div class="row">';
                var i;
                for (i = 0; i < links.length; i += 1) {
                    var link = articles[links[i]];
                    var linkhtml = '<div class="' + col + '">' +
                    '<div class="u-blog-thumb-v1">' +
                    '<a class="media d-flex align-items-center" href="/blog/articles/' + link.name + '/">' +
                    '<div class="u-blog-overlay-v2" style="background-image: url(/blog/articles/' + link.name +'/picture.jpg);"></div>' +
                    '<span class="media-body ml-3">' +
                    '<small class="d-block text-white mb-0">' + link.title + '</small>' +
                    '</span>' +
                    '</a>' +
                    '</div>' +
                    '</div>';
                    html += linkhtml;
                }

                html += '</div>';
                $(this).html(html);
            });

            $('#blogrow').html(html);

            $('.lazy').Lazy();
        });

    $(document).on('click', 'a', function () {
        if ($(this).attr('href')) {
            if (typeof mixpanel === 'object') {
                mixpanel.track('href ' + $(this).attr('href'));
            }
            if (typeof _gaq === 'object') {
                _gaq.push(['_trackPageview', 'href ' + $(this).attr('href')]);
            }
        }
    });
    if (typeof mixpanel === 'object') {
        mixpanel.track('Page ' + location.pathname);
    }

            console.log('defaults', defaults[id.split('-')[1]]);

            let settings = defaults[id.split('-')[1]];
            for (let k in settings) {
                if (typeof settings[k] === 'boolean') {
                    $('form#solution-form #' + k).prop('checked', settings[k]);
                } else {
                    $('form#solution-form #' + k).val(String(settings[k]));
                }
            }

            if (settings) {
                new Custombox.modal({
                    content: {
                        effect: 'blur',
                        target: '#defaultsmodal'
                    }
                }).open();
            } else {
                new Custombox.modal({
                    content: {
                        effect: 'blur',
                        target: '#genericmodal'
                    }
                }).open();
            }
        }

        $("form#solution-form :input").each(function() {
            if($(this).prop('id').length > 0) {
                let prop = {};
                let checked = $(this).prop('checked');
                if (checked !== undefined) {
                    prop.checked = checked;
                }
                let val = $(this).val();
                if (val !== 'on') {
                    prop.val = val;
                }
                selection[$(this).prop('id')] = prop;
            }
        });

        /* There must be at least one checkbox checked for us to show the "get result" button */
        let trues = 0;
        for (let k in selection) {
            if (selection[k].checked === true) {
                trues++;
            }
        }

        if (trues > 0) {
            $('.btn-result').removeClass('disabled');
        } else {
            $('.btn-result').addClass('disabled');
        }

    });
    $('.btn-result').addClass('disabled');

    function getselection() {
        let selection = {};


        $("form#solution-form :input").each(function() {
            if($(this).prop('id').length > 0) {
                let prop = {};
                let checked = $(this).prop('checked');
                if (checked !== undefined) {
                    prop.checked = checked;
                }
                let val = $(this).val();
                if (val !== 'on') {
                    prop.val = val;
                }
                selection[$(this).prop('id')] = prop;
            }
        });

        let usecase;
        for (let k in selection) {
            if (k.indexOf('usecase-') === 0 && selection[k].checked === true) {
                usecase = k.split('-')[1];
                break;
            }
        }
        if (usecase === undefined) {
            $('#pills-usecase-warning').show();
            $([document.documentElement, document.body]).animate({
                scrollTop: $("#solution-planner").offset().top - 100
            }, 1000);
            return;
        }
        if (usecase === 'none') {
            /* Check if there are any other selections done. If not, signal an error */
            let numselections = 0;
            for (let k in selection) {
                if (selection[k].checked === true) {
                    numselections++;
                }
            }
            console.log('numselections', numselections);
            if (numselections === 0) {
                $('#pills-usecase-warning').show();
                $([document.documentElement, document.body]).animate({
                    scrollTop: $("#solution-planner").offset().top - 100
                }, 1000);
                return;
            }
        }
        return selection
    }
    $('.btn-result').click(function (e) {

        function plan(selection, callback) {

           let url = 'https://5vr4zg9zq0.execute-api.us-east-1.amazonaws.com/dev/plan';
            if (location.host.indexOf('127.0.0.1') === 0) {
                url = 'http://localhost:3000/plan';
            }
            $.ajax({
                url: url,
                type: 'POST',
                contentType: 'application/json',
                data: JSON.stringify(selection),
                success: function (data) {
                    callback(data);
                }
            });
        }

        e.preventDefault();

        if (!$(this).hasClass('disabled')) {

            if (typeof _gaq === 'object') {
                _gaq.push(['_trackPageview', '/plan']);
            }

            selection = getselection();
            if (selection === undefined) {
                return;
            }

            $('#spinnermodal').modal('show');
            $('#pills-usecase-warning').hide();


            plan(selection, function (data) {

                console.log('data', data);
                $('#result-approx-time').html(data.time);
                $('#result-start-date').html(data.start);
                $('#result-end-date').html(data.end);
                $('#result-description').html(data.description);

                $('#result-soc-devices').html(data.socdevices);
                $('#result-soc-aps').html(data.socaps);
                if (data.socextenders) {
                    $('#result-soc-extenders').html(data.socextenders);
                    $('#result-extenders').show();
                } else {
                    $('#result-extenders').hide();
                }

                if (data.socgateways) {
                    $('#result-soc-gateways').html(data.socgateways);
                    $('#result-gateways').show();
                } else {
                    $('#result-gateways').hide();
                }

                let milestoneshtml = '';
                for (let m in data.milestones) {
                    milestoneshtml += '<li class="timeline-item bg-white rounded ml-3 p-4 shadow">' +
                    '<div class="timeline-arrow"></div>' +
                    '<h2 class="h5 mb-0">Milestone ' + (1 + Number(m)) + ': ' + data.milestones[m].title + '</h2>' +
                    '<span class="small text-gray">' +
                    data.milestones[m].date +
                    '</span>' +
                    '<p class="text-small mt-2 font-weight-light">' +
                    data.milestones[m].text +
                    '</li>';
                }
                $('#result-milestones').html(milestoneshtml);

                setTimeout(function () {
                    /*$('#pills-result-tab').removeClass('disabled');
                    $('#pills-result-tab').trigger('click');*/
                }, 800);
                setTimeout(function () {
                    $('#spinnermodal').modal('hide');

                }, 1500);
                $([document.documentElement, document.body]).animate({
                    scrollTop: $("#solution-planner").offset().top - 100
                }, 1000);
            });
        }
     });
    $('.btn-send').click(function (e) {

        function send(selection, callback) {

            let url = 'https://5vr4zg9zq0.execute-api.us-east-1.amazonaws.com/dev/plan';
            if (location.host.indexOf('127.0.0.1') === 0) {
                url = 'http://localhost:3000/plan';
            }

            selection.sendemail = true;
            $.ajax({
                url: url,
                type: 'POST',
                contentType: 'application/json',
                data: JSON.stringify(selection),
                success: function (data) {
                    callback(data);
                }
            });
        }

        e.preventDefault();

        selection = getselection();
        if (selection === undefined) {
            return;
        }

        if (typeof _gaq === 'object') {
            _gaq.push(['_trackPageview', '/send']);
        }

        $('#spinnermodal').modal('show');
        $('#pills-usecase-warning').hide();

        send(selection, function (data) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                $('#spinnermodal').modal('hide');
                new Custombox.modal({
                    content: {
                        effect: 'blur',
                        target: '#thanksmodal'
                    }
                }).open();
            }, 1500);
        });

    });

    $(document).on('change', '.custombox-content .get-success-story-accept', function (e) {
        if (this.checked) {
            $('.custombox-content a.get-success-story').removeClass('disabled');
        } else {
            $('.custombox-content a.get-success-story').addClass('disabled');
        }
    });

    $(document).on('click', '.custombox-content a.get-success-story', function (e) {

        let first = $('.custombox-content input[name="get-success-story-first"]').val();
        let last = $('.custombox-content input[name="get-success-story-last"]').val();
        let email = $('.custombox-content input[name="get-success-story-email"]').val();
        let casename = $('.custombox-content input[name="get-success-story-case"]').val();
        let title = $('.custombox-content input[name="get-success-story-title"]').val();
        let consent = $('.custombox-content .get-success-story-consent-text').html();

        e.preventDefault();

        if (typeof _gaq === 'object') {
            _gaq.push(['_trackPageview', '/get-success-story']);
        }

        var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
        var url = 'https://api.hsforms.com/submissions/v3/integration/submit/6754200/5f115629-d7a7-43e1-8bdb-605ac5d526ca';


        var data = {
            "submittedAt": Date.now(),
            "fields": [
            {
                "name": "email",
                "value": email
            },
            {
                "name": "firstname",
                "value": first
            },
            {
                "name": "lastname",
                "value": last
            },
            {
                "name": "case",
                "value": casename
            }

            ],
            "legalConsentOptions":{ // Include this object when GDPR options are enabled
                "consent":{
                    "consentToProcess":true,
                    "text": consent,
                    "communications":[
                    {
                        "value":true,
                        "subscriptionTypeId":999,
                        "text": consent
                    }
                    ]
                }
            }
        };

        var final_data = JSON.stringify(data);

        xhr.open('POST', url);
        xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json');

        Custombox.modal.close();
        $('#spinnermodal').modal('show');


        function error(msg) {
            console.log(msg);
            alert(msg);
        }

        xhr.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if(xhr.readyState == 4 && xhr.status == 200) {
                $('#spinnermodal').modal('hide');
                new Custombox.modal({
                    content: {
                        effect: 'blur',
                        target: '#downloadmodal'
                    }
                }).open();

                var link = document.createElement('a');
                link.href = '/download/cases/' + casename + '.pdf';
                link.download = 'Thingsquare success story ' + title + '.pdf';
                link.click();
                link.remove();

            } else if (xhr.readyState == 4 && xhr.status == 400){
                error(xhr.responseText); // Returns a 400 error the submission is rejected.
            } else if (xhr.readyState == 4 && xhr.status == 403){
                error(xhr.responseText); // Returns a 403 error if the portal isn't allowed to post submissions.
            } else if (xhr.readyState == 4 && xhr.status == 404){
                error(xhr.responseText); //Returns a 404 error if the formGuid isn't found
            }
        };

        xhr.send(final_data);

    });

</script>
